***achtste.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:achtste.html>achtste</a> (6972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ste</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">superlative</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Displaced <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">achtende</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ahtundo</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <i>-n-</i> by analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sivondo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seventh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nigundo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ninth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. An <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> older form <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:achten.html>achte</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:achtte.html>achtte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ahtodo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahtudô</i>.

***achttien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:achttien.html>achttien</a> (4518)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*achtetien</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*<a href = vnd.unilang:achttien.html>achttien</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ahtotēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ahtotien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahtōutehun</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">achttjin</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">achtzehn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eighteen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">atten</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actie</a></i>, directly or ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">āctiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">action</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:acties.html>acties</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">actiën</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>action, activity, movement; especially <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">without article</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> a fast-paced activity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> action; motion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> natuurkundeleraar <a href = vnd.unilang:demonstreerde.html>demonstreerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reactie.html>reactie</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klas.html>klas</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The physics teacher demonstrated the law of <b>action</b> and reaction in class.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> legal charge; formal claim</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> share in an enterprise
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aandeel.html>aandeel</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gerechtelijke.html>gerechtelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:acties.html>acties</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erfgenamen.html>erfgenamen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betroffen.html>betroffen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdeling.html>verdeling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b>actiën</b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:wijlen.html>wijlen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaders.html>vaders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The heirs' legal claims in court concerned the division of the <b>shares</b> in their late father's firm.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The plural form <i>actiën</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> archaic and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no longer used in the meaning “action”. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> however still used in historical contexts for the sense “share”.
</p>

***actieradius.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:actieradius.html>actieradius</a> (77530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:actie.html>actie</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">radius</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:actieradius.html>actieradius</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:actieradius.html>actieradii</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">actieradiussen</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>radius of action <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">radius or range in which something operate, or where a vehicle, vessel or aircraft can reach</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adam.html>Adam</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:adam.html>Adam</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kostuum.html>kostuum</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">suit, costume</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> add (313)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>add</b>

***adel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:adel.html>adel</a> (8867)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:adel.html>adel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*athal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aþalą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adel.html>adel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>nobility</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***adelaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:adelaar.html>adelaar</a> (9394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">adeler</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Adler</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaar.html>adelaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaars.html>adelaars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaar.html>adelaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eagle (Any of several large carnivorous <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> in the family Accipitridae)</li>
<li>effigy of an eagle; insignia comprising one
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Romeinse <a href = vnd.unilang:legioenen.html>legioenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koesteren.html>koesterden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaars.html>adelaars</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> Britse <a href = vnd.unilang:regimenten.html>regimenten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:banieren.html>banieren</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Roman legions treasured their <b>eagles</b> like British regiments treasured their colours.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> eagle (on or supporting a coat of arms)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Duitsland, <a href = vnd.unilang:polen.html>Polen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Roemenië <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:adelaars.html>adelaars</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wapens.html>wapens</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Germany, Poland and Romania all have <b>eagles</b> on their <a href = vnd.unilang:coats.html>coats</a> of arms.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adel.html>adel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nobility</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stand</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">estate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adelstand.html>adelstand</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adelstand.html>adelstanden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adelstand.html>adelstandje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The aristocracy as a socially privileged estate, the nobility.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:sommige.html>sommige</a> statenvergaderingen gold <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:adel.html>adel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> stand, in <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> geestelijkheid.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In some feudal estates the nobility ranked as first estate, in other the clergy.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The status of being considered nobility.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âdem</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*āthom</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ēþmaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li>breath</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***adieu.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:adieu.html>adieu</a> (16732)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">adiu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>. <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>Later</a> reinfluenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:adieu.html>adieu</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_2">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adieu.html>adieu</a></strong>
